Unknown option. Please review accepted flags.
Script to submit conversions from gpubox files to uvfits with van Vleck corrections,
make WODEN simulations, make flagging cuts, and transfer to Ozstar
All binary options require a 1 to be passed to be activated, i.e. -o 1

Syntax: nohup ./limit_pipeline.sh [-o -d -p -a -c -b -t -g -w -n -m -C] >> ~/log.txt &
options:
-o (text file with observation list, required), 
-w (wallclock time, default=5:00:00), 
-n (number of slots, default=1), 
-m (memory allocation, default=120G), 
-C (check for outputs, print missing obs,  and exit),

nohup ./uvfits_pipeline.sh -o /astro/mwaeor/nbarry/van_vleck_corrected/2014_2.txt -d /astro/mwaeor/MWA/data/ -p /astro/mwaeor/nbarry/van_vleck_corrected/coarse_corr_no_ao/ -a 0 -c 1 -b 1 -t 1 -g 1
